### [1] [Physics-Informed Neural Networks for Solving Two-Flavor Neutrino Oscillations in Vacuum and Matter Environments for Atmospheric and Reactor Neutrinos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22862)
*Srinivasan T.,Kalyani Desikan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出使用物理信息神经网络（PINN）求解中微子在真空和物质中的演化微分方程，精度媲美解析解，且具备免网格、高维简化与复杂几何适应性等优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中微子振荡是粒子物理关键课题，传统数值方法在复杂介质或高维场景中存在局限，亟需更灵活高效的求解工具。

Method: 基于中微子振荡理论框架（含真空混合与MSW效应），构建物理信息神经网络（PINN）模型，分别求解真空及恒定密度物质中的中微子演化方程。

Result: PINN对反应堆（低能）和大气（高能）中微子演化模拟达到10^{-3}–10^{-4}量级的均方误差，精度接近解析解；验证了其在免网格、高维降维和复杂几何建模方面的可行性。

Conclusion: PINN为中微子演化问题提供了高精度、免网格的新数值范式，具备向三味中微子及非均匀物质分布等更复杂场景拓展的潜力。

Abstract: Neutrino oscillations provide crucial insights into fundamental particle physics, with two-flavor approximations effectively describing reactor and atmospheric phenomena. This paper explores the use of Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) to solve the governing differential equations for neutrino evolution in both vacuum and matter environments. We review the theoretical framework, including vacuum mixing and the Mikheyev-Smirnov-Wolfenstein (MSW) effect in matter, and demonstrate PINN implementations for vacuum and constant-density profiles. This Machine learning based approach for reactor (low-energy) and atmospheric (high-energy) neutrinos shows high precision similar to analytical solutions, with mean squared errors of the order of \(10^{-3}-10^{-4)\). Although this work focuses on solving the evolution equation in general cases, we discuss the significant potential advantages of PINNs over traditional solvers, without any mesh requirements, high-dimensionality reduction, and applicability to complex geometries, along with future extensions to three-flavor effects.

</details>


### [2] [Dalitz Plot Kinematics for a Lorentz-Violating Three-Body Decay](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22867)
*Joshua O'Connor*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文分析了洛伦兹破缺量子场论中三粒子相互作用和衰变过程的领头阶修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究洛伦兹对称性破缺对多粒子过程的影响，以检验基础物理理论的普适性。

Method: 在洛伦兹破缺量子场论框架下，计算三粒子相互作用和衰变过程的领头阶修正。

Result: 给出了三粒子过程在洛伦兹破缺背景下的修正形式。

Conclusion: 洛伦兹破缺可导致三粒子相互作用和衰变过程出现可观测的领头阶修正，为实验检验提供理论依据。

Abstract: We outline the analysis of three-particle interactions and decay processes for leading-order modifications in a Lorentz-violating quantum field theory.

</details>


### [3] [Three regimes/phases of QCD at high T, their symmetries and N_c scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23689)
*L. Ya. Glozman*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文综述了小化学势下QCD相图在温度升高时的最新进展，划分了三个不同对称性、自由度和N_c标度的相：手征恢复温度以下的强子气、手征恢复与退禁闭温度之间的弦状流体、以及退禁闭温度以上的夸克胶子等离子体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解QCD在不同温度和化学势下的相结构及其演化规律，特别是小化学势高温度区域的相变行为。

Method: 综述性分析，基于对称性、自由度和N_c标度等理论特征对QCD相图进行分相描述。

Result: 明确了QCD在小化学势高温区域存在三个典型相：强子气、弦状流体和夸克胶子等离子体，并给出了各相的温度边界。

Conclusion: QCD相图在小化学势高温区可由手征恢复与退禁闭两个关键温度划分为三个物理性质迥异的相，反映了强相互作用物质在极端条件下的丰富结构。

Abstract: We review recent developments on the QCD phase diagram at small chemical potentials and increasing temperature. There are three regimes/phases in QCD which differ by symmetries, degrees of freedom and N_c scaling: the hadron gas below the chiral restoration temperature T_ch, the stringy fluid between T_ch and the deconfinement temperature T_d and the quark-gluon plasma above T_d.

</details>


### [4] [Amplitude-Based Analysis of QED Radiative Corrections to Electroproduction of $η$-Mesons on Protons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22943)
*Isabella Illari,Andrei Afanasev,William J. Briscoe,Victor L. Kashevarov,Axel Schmidt,Igor I. Strakovsky*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了η介子电生过程辐射修正的理论形式，并利用EXCLURAD程序结合EtaMAID-2023多极振幅进行了数值计算，发现辐射修正因子在共振区可达约30%，且对光束自旋不对称性有15–25%的压制效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为精确提取η介子电生过程中的共振结构信息（如S11(1535)和S11(1650)），需对实验数据进行可靠的辐射修正，而此前该通道缺乏系统的形式化处理。

Method: 基于已有的π介子电生辐射修正框架，拓展建立η介子电生的辐射修正形式；采用EXCLURAD代码并输入EtaMAID-2023多极振幅进行数值计算。

Result: 在W=1.49–2.0 GeV共振区，辐射修正因子δ最大达~30%，峰值出现在W≈1.66 GeV；光束自旋不对称性被压制15–25%；提供了Q²=0.3–4.0 GeV²及全角度范围的数值结果，适用于JLab CLAS12实验。

Conclusion: 该辐射修正形式及数值结果为CLAS12上η介子电生实验的数据分析提供了关键工具，有助于提升对N*共振性质的精确测定。

Abstract: A formalism for radiative correction calculations in exclusive $η$ electroproduction on the proton is presented, extending the treatment developed for the pion channel. The EXCLURAD code is used in the radiative correction procedure with EtaMAID-2023 multipole amplitudes. The cross-section correction factor $δ$ varies by up to ${\sim}\,30\%$ across the resonance region $W = 1.49$-$2.0$ GeV at $E_{\rm beam} = 6.535$ GeV, with a local maximum near $W \simeq 1.66$ GeV driven by the $S_{11}(1535)$ and $S_{11}(1650)$ resonances. The beam-spin asymmetry is suppressed by 15-25% at the same kinematics. Numerical results covering $Q^2 = 0.3$-$4.0$ GeV$^2$ and the full angular range are provided for kinematics relevant to CLAS12 experiments at Jefferson Lab.

</details>


### [5] [Light-front mass operator with dressed quarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22953)
*J. A. O. Marinho,J. P. B. C. de Melo,T. Frederico,W. de Paula*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个包含夸克修饰效应的有效光前质量平方算符，用于夸克-反夸克系统，并将其应用于介子结构研究，特别是π介子的横向动量依赖分布、部分子分布函数和分布振幅的计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将非微扰QCD动力学纳入光前哈密顿方法描述强子结构中，解决夸克修饰效应在光前框架下的处理问题。

Method: 基于格点QCD启发的闵可夫斯基空间夸克传播子，推导轻夸克-反夸ark系统的光前分离型预解式；采用广义谱表示分离瞬时贡献，并投影到组分夸克螺旋度基上，得到有效修饰的质量平方算符；引入有效光前夸克自能并分析其动量依赖性。

Result: 夸克修饰效应引起显著的红外修正，同时保持可控的紫外行为；成功计算了π介子的横向动量依赖分布、无极化部分子分布函数和分布振幅。

Conclusion: 该框架为在光前哈密顿方法中系统纳入非微扰QCD效应提供了可行路径，提升了对强子结构尤其是低能区性质的理论描述能力。

Abstract: We construct an effective light-front mass-squared operator for quark-antiquark systems that incorporates quark dressing effects through a running quark mass. Starting from a Minkowski-space quark propagator constrained by lattice-QCD-inspired parametrization, we derive the disconnected light-front resolvent for a light quark-antiquark system using a generalized spectral representation of an individual quark propagator separating out the instantaneous contributions. By projecting the resolvent onto a constituent-quark helicity basis, we obtain an effective dressed mass-squared operator suitable for light-front Hamiltonian approaches. We introduce an effective light-front quark self-energy and analyze its momentum dependence. As an application, we study pion structure using representative light-front wave-function models and compute unpolarized transverse-momentum-dependent distributions, unpolarized parton distribution functions and distribution amplitudes. Our results show that quark dressing induces sizable infrared modifications while preserving controlled ultraviolet behavior, providing a framework to incorporate nonperturbative QCD dynamics into light-front descriptions of hadrons.

</details>


### [6] [Mono-Z' Signatures in the B-L Supersymmetric Standard Model at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23038)
*Ali Cici,Shaaban Khalil,Stefano Moretti,Cem Salih Un*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了B-L超对称标准模型（BLSSM-IS）中Z'玻色子与单态希格斯h'联合产生过程，其中h'衰变为不可见的轻质量超对称粒子（LSP）对，构成暗物质候选者；通过分析末态轻子和缺失横向能量的运动学分布，提出一种不依赖于具体暗物质成分的信号提取方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在BLSSM-IS框架下，Z'玻色子质量受LHC实验限制较紧（约2.2 TeV），且存在与标准模型的干涉效应；同时需发展对暗物质性质不敏感的探测策略。

Method: 聚焦Z'的轻子衰变道（e/μ），分析末态轻子动量、角度及缺失横向能量（MET）的运动学分布，以区分信号与背景。

Result: 提出了基于运动学分布的mono-Z'信号提取方法，该方法不依赖于LSP是中性微子还是右手中微子超伴子的具体身份。

Conclusion: 该分析为BLSSM-IS模型中Z'-h'联合产生及不可见衰变提供了通用且可行的LHC探测途径，增强了对B-L扩展超对称模型的实验检验能力。

Abstract: The B-L Supersymmetric Standard Model with Inverse Seesaw (BLSSM-IS) extends the Minimal Supersymmetric Standard Model (MSSM) by incorporating a gauged B-L symmetry, right-handed neutrinos and an additional neutral gauge boson Z'. Searches at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) constrain the mass of this gauge boson to be as low as only ~ 2.2 TeV in the BLSSM-IS, owing to interference effects with the SM. In this framework, mono-Z' events can arise from the associated production of a Z' boson and a singlet Higgs boson h', where h' subsequently decays into missing energy carried by a pair of the Lightest Supersymmetric Particle (LSP) - either a neutralino or a right-handed sneutrino - which serves as a Dark Matter (DM) candidate. Focusing on leptonic decays of the Z' (electrons and muons), we analyse the kinematic distributions of the final-state leptons and the missing transverse energy in order to extract a signal for this process which is independent of the nature of the BLSSM-IS DM.

</details>


### [7] [$D\bar{D}^\ast$-$πJ/ψ$ scatterings of coupled channels for $Z_c(3900)$ channel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23078)
*Yukihiro Abe,Yasuhiro Yamaguchi,Atsushi Hosaka*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过耦合通道分析研究了Zc(3900)共振态，发现短程夸克交换（特别是DD*与J/ψπ之间的跃迁）是主导散射振幅的关键机制，而介子交换势贡献较小，该结论与HALQCD格点模拟结果一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解Zc(3900)这一类奇特强子态的内部结构和产生机制，尤其是区分介子分子态与紧致四夸克态等不同图像。

Method: 在强子-夸克有效模型框架下，对DD*、J/ψπ等相关介子对进行耦合通道分析，包含π和D(*)介子交换势以及夸克交换相互作用。

Result: 介子交换势较弱，而DD*与J/ψπ之间的短程夸克交换相互作用很强，主导Zc(3900)通道的散射振幅，并与HALQCD格点QCD模拟结果一致。

Conclusion: Zc(3900)的形成主要源于DD*与J/ψπ通道间的强短程夸克交换效应，支持其具有显著的四夸克或夸克-胶子混合成分，而非纯介子分子态。

Abstract: We perform coupled channel analysis for $D \bar D^*$, $J/ψπ$ and related meson pairs for the $Z_c(3900)$ channel in an effective model of hadrons and quarks. The model incorporates meson exchange potential such as one pion and $D^{(*)}$ meson exchanges, and quark exchanges. It turns out that the meson exchange potential is small, while the off-diagonal interactions by the quark exchanges at short distances, particularly for transitions between $D\bar D^*$-$J/ψπ$ are strong, which plays a main role for the scattering amplitudes for the $Z_c(3900)$ channel, in consistent with the results of the lattice simulations of the HALQCD group.

</details>


### [8] [Baryon enhancement in jets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23189)
*Antonio Ortiz,Robert Vertesi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文报告了在13 TeV pp碰撞中，当喷注横动量大于15 GeV/c时，重子产额相对于介子的增强现象，并指出该效应源于夸克引发喷注向胶子引发喷注的转变，挑战了基于集体流和夸克复合机制的传统解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重子相对于介子的产额增强在小碰撞系统中是一个突破性发现，传统上该效应在重离子碰撞中被归因于强相互作用夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）的形成；因此需探究其在pp碰撞中的物理起源。

Method: 利用PYTHIA8模拟13 TeV pp碰撞中横动量大于15 GeV/c的带电粒子喷注，并分析重子/介子比随喷注多重数的变化，结合夸克与胶子引发喷注的区分进行物理解释。

Result: 观测到高横动量喷注中显著的重子增强效应，并发现该效应与喷注多重数相关，可由夸克引发（低多重数）向胶子引发（高多重数）喷注的过渡合理解释。

Conclusion: 该重子增强并非源于类似重离子碰撞中的集体膨胀或夸克重组机制，而更可能源自初态部分子类型（夸克vs胶子）及其碎裂特性的差异，从而对小系统中QGP类效应的解释提出挑战。

Abstract: The enhancement of the baryon production relative to mesons in small-collision systems is considered a breakthrough result of the Large Hadron Collider since a similar effect in heavy-ion collisions is understood by invoking the formation of the strongly-interacting quark--gluon plasma. In this letter, a baryon enhancement is reported for $p_{\rm T}^{\rm ch,\, jet}>15$\,GeV/$c$ jets produced in pp collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13$\,TeV simulated with PYTHIA8. The effect can be explained as a transition between quark-initiated jets (low jet multiplicities) to gluon-initiated jets (high jet multiplicities). The present result challenges the interpretation about the multiplicity dependence of the baryon enhancement in terms of collective expansion of the medium and quark recombination.

</details>


### [9] [Coupled-channel study of the three-body $DDK$ and $D^{*}D^{*}K$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23298)
*Hai-Peng Xie,Si-Yi Chen,Ning Li,Wei Chen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有量子数 I(J^P) = 1/2(0⁻) 的三体 DDK 系统，采用耦合通道框架（包含 DDK 和 D*D*K 构型），结合单玻色子交换模型与手征有效理论描述相互作用，并用高斯展开法和复标度法求解；结果发现 DDK 系统存在一个深束缚态和可能的浅束缚态（具晕结构），但未发现共振极点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索含粲介子与K介子的少体系统动力学，特别是基于分子态解释（如Ds0*(2317)）和格点QCD约束，理解DDK三体系统的束缚态与共振行为。

Method: 采用耦合通道框架，包含DDK和D*D*K构型；DD(*)D(*)相互作用由符合重夸克对称性的单玻色子交换模型描述，并拟合X(3872)、Tcc+、Zc(3900)极点；DK相互作用来自手征有效理论并受格点QCD散射长度约束；三体问题用高斯展开法求解，复标度法搜寻共振态。

Result: DDK系统支持一个在宽参数范围内稳定的深束缚态（紧凑三体结构）；在DK相互作用长程行为适当时，还可能出现靠近D-DK阈值的浅束缚态（具三体晕特征）；D*D*K耦合通道效应可忽略；未在所考察参数区域内发现明确共振极点；D*D*K系统也得到类似结论。

Conclusion: DDK系统倾向于形成束缚态而非共振态，深束缚态稳定存在，浅束缚态依赖于DK相互作用细节；该工作为理解含粲介子- kaon 少体系统提供了新见解，暗示此类系统中可能存在新颖的强子结构。

Abstract: We investigate the three-body $DDK$ system with quantum numbers $I(J^P) = \frac{1}{2}(0^-)$ within a coupled-channel framework that incorporates both $DDK$ and $D^{*}D^{*}K$ configurations. The $D^{(*)}D^{(*)}$ interactions are described using the one-boson-exchange model constrained by the heavy-quark symmetry and fitted to the pole positions of $X(3872)$, $T_{cc}^+$, and $Z_c(3900)$. The $D^{(*)}K$ interaction is from the chiral effective theory, motivated by the molecular interpretation of $D_{s0}^*(2317)$, and is further constrained by lattice-QCD results for the $DK$ scattering lengths. The resulting three-body problem is solved using the Gaussian expansion method, while the complex scaling method is employed to search for possible resonant states. We find that coupled-channel effects from $D^{*}D^{*}K$ are negligible, and the $DDK$ system supports a deeply bound state across a wide range of parameters. Depending on the long-range behavior of the $DK$ interaction, an additional shallow state may emerge near the particle-dimer ($D$-$DK$) threshold. The deeply bound state exhibits a compact three-body structure, whereas the shallow state displays characteristic features of a three-body halo configuration. No clear resonance poles are identified within the explored parameter region. Similar results are obtained for the $D^{*}D^{*}K$ system. These findings may provide new insight into few-body dynamics in systems involving charmed mesons and kaons.

</details>


### [10] [Two-loop quarkonium Hamiltonian in annihilation channel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23303)
*Yukinari Sumino,Takahiro Ueda*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在potential-NRQCD有效场论框架下计算了湮灭道的两圈夸克偶素哈密顿量，并与先前NRQCD中四夸克算符的结果一致；进一步推广至一般色结构，适用于其他规范群；结合非湮灭道的两圈结果，完成了完整的两圈夸克偶素哈密顿量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 完成夸克偶素两圈哈密顿量的完整计算，拓展其适用规范群范围。

Method: 基于potential-NRQCD有效场论，计算湮灭道两圈贡献，并推广色结构。

Result: 得到湮灭道两圈哈密顿量，与NRQCD四夸克算符结果一致，并给出适用于一般规范群的色结构表达式；结合非湮灭道结果，完成全两圈哈密顿量。

Conclusion: 本文完成了夸克偶素两圈哈密顿量的完整构造，提升了理论精度并扩展了适用性。

Abstract: We calculate the two-loop quarkonium Hamiltonian in the annihilation channel within the framework of potential-NRQCD effective field theory. The result agrees with the previous calculation of the corresponding four-quark operator in NRQCD for SU(N) color gauge group. We further obtain an expression with a more general color structure applicable to other gauge groups. Combined with the recently calculated two-loop Hamiltonian in the non-annihilation channel, this completes the full two-loop quarkonium Hamiltonian.

</details>


### [11] [Some approximate renormalization group invariants for supersymmetric extensions of the Standard Model and the Yukawa unification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23329)
*Kirill Krylov,Daniil Rystsov,Konstantin Stepanyantz*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建了包含第三代和第二代Yukawa耦合的近似重整化群不变量，用于分析大统一尺度下的Yukawa耦合关系，并提出引入SU(5)五重态超场可实现Yukawa统一，暗示潜在E6规范对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超对称标准模型中Yukawa耦合在大统一尺度下的可能统一关系，并解释实验观测的粒子质量。

Method: 构造对量子修正不敏感的Yukawa耦合组合（近似RG不变量），结合MSSM扩展（加入5+5̅超场），分析其在M_X尺度的耦合关系及对tgβ和α(M_X)的预测。

Result: 发现引入SU(5)五重态超场后，第二、三代Yukawa耦合可在M_X实现统一，且与实验粒子质量兼容；该结构暗示潜在的E6大统一规范对称性。

Conclusion: Yukawa统一可通过扩展MSSM实现，所提出的不变量为检验大统一理论（尤其是E6）提供了新工具和约束。

Abstract: For supersymmetric extensions of the Standard Model we construct some expressions that include Yukawa couplings for the third and second generations and receive relatively small quantum corrections. This implies that they slightly depend on scale and are therefore approximate renormalization group invariants. Using these invariants we try to analyse possible relations between the Yukawa couplings at the unification scale $M_X$ as well as the predictions for values of $\mbox{tg}\,β$ and $α(M_X)$. In particular, we suggest two variants of such relations and investigate whether they agree with the experimental values of elementary particle masses. It is demonstrated that the Yukawa unification for the third and second generations consistent with them can be achieved by adding exotic superfields forming 3 representations $5+\bar{5}$ of the group $SU(5)$ to the MSSM field content. We argue that this may indicate the possible underlying $E_6$ gauge symmetry.

</details>


### [12] [Possible Evidence for Neutral Color-Singlet $q\bar q$ Quark Matter from High-Energy Pb-Emulsion Collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23473)

<details>

Method: 将实验观测的e⁺e⁻谱特征（宽增强、3±1 MeV、7±1 MeV、19±1 MeV等共振）与理论模型对比：宽增强归因于QED(U(1)）去禁闭夸克-反夸克热湮灭（相变温度T_c(QED)≈4.75±1.2 MeV）；低质量共振解释为去禁闭d d̄、u ū库仑束缚态；19 MeV峰解释为QED(U(1)）禁闭的中性介子。

Result: 理论预测的T_c(QED)与宽增强位置、各共振峰质量与对应夸克束缚态/介子质量大致吻合，表明实验中可能同时产生了QED(U(1)）禁闭与去禁闭的中性无色q q̄夸克物质。

Abstract: The invariant mass spectrum of $e^+e^-$ pairs produced in high-energy Pb-emulsion collisions at 160 A GeV at CERN SPS exhibits a complex structure of many resonances resting on top of a broad enhancement at invariant masses below 50 MeV, with the prominent resonance at 19 $\pm$1 MeV providing independent support for the hypothetical X17 particle. We show that this complex structure may be coherently described as signatures for the neutral color-singlet $q\bar q$ quark matter in both its deconfined and confined phases. That is, the broad enhancement may arise from thermal annihilation of QED(U(1))-deconfined quarks and antiquarks into $e^+e^-$ pairs at the phase transition temperature $T_c$(QED), theoretically estimated to be 4.75 $\pm$ 1.2 MeV from the transitional equilibrium condition. The observed 3$\pm$1 and 7$\pm$1 MeV resonances may correspond to the QED(U(1))-deconfined $d\bar d$ and $u\bar u$ Coulomb bound states near their quark rest masses, respectively, whereas the observed 19 $\pm$ 1 MeV resonance may correspond to the QED(U(1))-confined isoscalar QED meson. The approximate agreement between the theoretical and the experimental spectrum suggests that both QED(U(1))-confined and QED(U(1))-deconfined neutral color-singlet $q\bar q$ quark matter may have been produced in these high-energy Pb-emulsion collisions. We propose future experiments to confirm or refute these findings.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确确定K介子分布振幅对理解强子结构及QCD非微扰动力学至关重要，而传统格点QCD难以直接计算光锥分布振幅，因此需借助LaMET框架从准分布振幅外推。

Method: 基于2+1味泛函QCD计算的欧氏空间夸克关联函数与K介子Bethe-Salpeter振幅，采用复动量平面的轮廓形变法提取大纵向动量下的准DA，并进行1/P_z^2和1/P_z^4阶外推以获取真实DA。

Conclusion: 该工作为K介子DA提供了基于第一性原理的可靠理论预测，验证了LaMET结合泛函QCD方法在介子结构研究中的可行性与精度。

Abstract: We study the kaon quasi-distribution amplitude (quasi-DA) and distribution amplitude (DA) within the large-momentum effective theory (LaMET) combined with the first-principles functional QCD. Using quark correlation functions and the kaon Bethe-Salpeter amplitude in the Euclidean space from the 2+1 flavour functional QCD [1] as inputs, we obtain the kaon quasi DA in the large longitudinal momentum region with the contour deformation method [2] in the complex plane of momentum. By performing $1/P_z^2$ and $1/P_z^4$ order extrapolations of the kaon quasi-DA for the choices of the maximal longitudinal momentum $P_z^{\max}\in[2,2.5]$ GeV, we obtain a single-peaked and asymmetric kaon DA with the uncertainties arising from the extrapolation interval and ansatz. We find the first and second order moments of the kaon DA, $\langle ξ\rangle_K = 0.020(3)$ and $\langle ξ^2 \rangle_K = 0.253(12)$, respectively.

Method: 基于超轻玻色子在宏观源附近产生的静态势，计算其在约瑟夫森结中引起的相位偏移，并通过精密电流测量实现探测；设计三种实验构型，分别对应光亲和标量、洛伦兹破缺标量和轴子介导的单极-偶极相互作用，依据源是否极化进行区分。

Abstract: Ultralight bosons sourced by macroscopic objects can generate long-range spin-independent and spin-dependent potentials that are accessible to precision interferometry. Such potentials induce phase shifts in Josephson junctions, detectable through precision current measurements. We propose three experimental scenarios to probe photophilic scalar interactions, Lorentz-violating scalar-mediated interactions, and axion-mediated monopole-dipole interactions, depending on the nature (unpolarized or polarized) of the source. The proposed setups provide sensitivities to novel mixed couplings that are largely unconstrained by existing bounds and enables the exploration of new forces at centimeter to micrometer length scales.

### [15] [Probing the electron Yukawa coupling via resonant Higgs boson production at FCC-ee via $e^+e^- \to H \to WW^*$ in lepton-plus-jets final states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24152)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于FCC-ee设计参数（√s=125 GeV、能量展宽4.1 MeV、积分亮度10 ab⁻¹），对e⁺e⁻→H→WW*→ℓ±ν+jj四种末态（含轻子和强子衰变）开展详细蒙特卡洛模拟；使用多类别梯度提升决策树（GBDT）结合运动学与拓扑变量进行信号/背景分类。

Result: 获得2.0σ的联合统计显著性，对应电子耦合修正因子上限κₑ ≲ 1.35（95% CL），是迄今模拟研究中对yₑ最严格的约束。

Conclusion: 该研究表明FCC-ee上的s通道希格斯产生是探测电子汤川耦合的有力途径，虽当前灵敏度尚未达发现水平，但为未来高精度测量奠定了方法学基础，并凸显了能量单色化与先进分类器的关键作用。

Abstract: We report a detailed simulation study of the search for $s$-channel Higgs boson production in $e^+e^-$ collisions at a center-of-mass (c.m.) energy of $\sqrt{s}=125\,\mathrm{GeV}$ at the CERN Future Circular Collider (FCC-ee), as a means to constrain the electron Yukawa coupling, $y_e$. The process of interest is $e^+e^-\to H\to WW^*\to \ell^\pmν+ jj$ with four different $WW^*$ final states considered, involving both on- and off-shell $W$ bosons decaying either into dileptons ($\ell^\pm = e^\pm$ and $μ^\pm$, including those from $τ^\pm$ decays) or into dijets ($jj$). Signal and background events are discriminated through a multiclass gradient boosted decision tree exploiting a comprehensive set of kinematic and topological variables across the four final-state categories. Assuming a monochromatized c.m. energy spread of 4.1 MeV, yielding a $σ_{e^+e^-\to H} = 280\,\mathrm{ab}$ resonant cross section, and an integrated luminosity of $10\,\mathrm{ab}^{-1}$, the analysis achieves a combined statistical significance of 2.0 standard deviations. This corresponds to an upper limit on the coupling modifier $κ_e = y_e/y_e^{\rm SM} \lesssim 1.35$ at 95\% confidence level, and provides the most stringent constraint on the electron Yukawa coupling achieved in simulation-based studies to date.

Abstract: This contribution reviews recent progress in the low-lying scalar mesons and glueballs. We propose a new classification for the scalar nonet that includes $f_0(980)$ and $a_0(980)$ as the lowest states, while we identify $f_0(1500)$ as a primary glueball candidate. We demonstrate that the production yields of these states in heavy-ion collisions are mutually consistent across statistical, coalescence, and S-matrix frameworks. To investigate their internal structure, we move beyond standard phenomenology by describing glueballs as topological solitons. This approach yields an energy spectrum in excellent agreement with lattice QCD and experimental data, while interpreting $f_0(2470)$ as a tightly bound glueballonium to explain its anomalously long lifetime. This non-perturbative framework provides a predictive basis for the future experimental verification of exotic scalar states.

### [17] [How to understand $ρ$ Resonance from the Quark Model and $ππ$ $P$-wave phase shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24270)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统组分夸克模型忽略强子通道耦合效应，难以准确描述ρ介子（强耦合ππ、大衰变宽度）的物理性质。

Method: 1) 用窄介子数据重新拟合手征夸克模型参数；2) 得到ρ介子裸质量作为强子层次输入；3) 基于逆散射理论构建裸态与ππ连续谱耦合模型，利用P波ππ散射相移提取相互作用，并计算宽度与裸态成分。

Result: 成功计算了ρ介子的衰变宽度及其物理态中的裸态成分，并验证了该框架对其他强通道耦合显著的强子共振也具普适性。

Abstract: As the lightest isovector vector meson, the $ρ$ meson is an important object for investigating the structure of resonant states in strong interactions. Owing to its strong coupling to the $ππ$ channel and its large decay width, the conventional constituent quark model treatment, in which it is simply regarded as a pure $q\bar q$ bound state while the hadronic-channel coupling effects are neglected, is insufficient to fully characterize its physical properties. To this end, in the present work we establish a unified framework for studying the structure and resonant properties of the $ρ$ meson by combining the quark-gluon and hadronic degrees of freedom. At the quark-gluon level, we first determine the parameters of the chiral quark model by refitting a set of narrow mesons for which open OZI-allowed strong-decay channels are absent or strongly suppressed. With these parameters fixed, the bare mass of the $ρ$ meson is obtained and used as the input for the subsequent hadronic-level analysis. At the hadronic level, based on inverse scattering theory, we construct a model including the coupling between the bare state and the $ππ$ continuum, extract the $ρ_0-ππ$ interaction using the $P$-wave $ππ$ scattering phase-shift data, and further calculate the width of the $ρ$ meson as well as the bare-state component in the physical state. The present work also provides a generalizable analytical framework for further studies of other hadronic resonances with significant channel-coupling effects.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We study the phenomenology of heavy neutral leptons (HNLs) in $B$-meson decays as probes of physics beyond the Standard Model. Focusing on the leptonic channels $B \to μN$ and $B \to τN$, we constrain the allowed regions in the $M_N$--$|U_{\ell N}|^2$ plane using current experimental data. Using these constraints, we investigate lepton-number violating ($ΔL=2$) processes mediated by on-shell HNLs, including $B_{(c)}^- \to π^+ μ^- μ^-$ and $B_c^- \to J/ψ\, π^+ μ^- μ^-$. For benchmark values $|U_{μN}|^2 = 10^{-6}$ and $M_N = 2$-- $3\,\mathrm{GeV}$, the predicted branching ratios lie in the range $\mathcal{O}(10^{-13})$--$\mathcal{O}(10^{-8})$. Among the channels, $B_c^- \to π^+ μ^- μ^-$ shows the largest enhancement, while $B_c^- \to J/ψ\, π^+ μ^- μ^-$ is strongly suppressed. These results indicate a clear channel dependence, with $B_c$ modes providing enhanced sensitivity to HNL effects and offering promising avenues for future searches of lepton number violation.

### [19] [CP violation in $Σ^+\to p\ell^+\ell^-$ within the standard model and beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24335)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 理论分析方法：基于标准模型框架，评估长程强子贡献所引入的吸收相位，并研究其与可能的新物理振幅干涉导致的CP破坏效应；同时拓展至Σ⁺→pe⁺e⁻和Σ⁺→pγ等关联衰变模式。

Result: 发现Σ⁺→pμ⁺μ⁻衰变中的CP不对称性（衰变率不对称）当前理论允许高达数十个百分点，LHCb可在近未来进行探测；类似结论也适用于Σ⁺→pe⁺e⁻和Σ⁺→pγ过程。

Abstract: The LHCb collaboration has recently observed the rare hyperon decay $Σ^+\to pμ^+μ^-$. It can also measure the corresponding antihyperon channel with comparable precision and is thus in a position to extract information on $CP$ violation in this mode. Interestingly, the long-distance contributions that dominate it within the standard model provide large absorptive phases that could drive substantial $CP$ violation through interference with potential new-physics contributions. Here we explore this possibility, finding that the decay rate asymmetry is currently allowed to be as high as tens of percent, which can be probed by LHCb in the near future. We additionally consider the same with regard to the dielectron mode $Σ^+\to pe^+e^-$ as well as the related radiative one $Σ^+\to pγ$.

</details>

Abstract: In this paper, we present the production of double SM-like Higgs $ (h) $ at the future electron positron colliders within the context of $ S_{3} $ model with three Higgs doublets (S3-3H) and no CP violation to describe beyond the Standard Model Higgs Physics. Finally, by revisiting the effects of statistical isotropy and causality on the spectrum, we define general correlation functions that are then fitted to the simulation data and compared to the analytic results.

Abstract: Both scalar and vector dark matter can be produced during a cosmological first order phase transition if the dark matter is coupled to the field undergoing the transition. Both kinds of particle are also produced by the plasma through the normal freeze out scenario. For dark matter particles in the traditional thermal relic GeV-TeV window, dark sector phase transitions around a GeV affect scalar dark matter and dark sector phase transitions around 10 MeV affect vector dark matter abundances (and therefore should take place in a dark sector). <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为改进重夸克在RHIC和LHC能量下的Langevin模拟，需更精确地刻画其在强磁场热QCD介质中的输运性质。

Abstract: Heavy quark (HQ) momentum ($κ$) and spatial diffusion ($D_s$) coefficients are computed in a non-perturbative thermal QCD medium in the presence of a background magnetic field of arbitrary strength. Both perturbative and non-perturbative effects are incorporated via the in-medium HQ potential, obtained from the resummed gluon propagator. We find that the momentum diffusion coefficients become anisotropic even in the static heavy quark limit, with the magnetic field direction defining the axis of anisotropy. This anisotropy originates from restrictions on longitudinal momentum diffusion in the gluon spectral function, and naturally leads to two spatial diffusion coefficients ($D_s^L$, $D_s^T$). Non-perturbative effects are found to be dominant at low temperatures. These results provide a more consistent input for Langevin based calculations of the heavy quark directed flow at RHIC and LHC energies.

### [25] [Mass spectra of charged mesons and the quenching of vector meson condensation via exact phase-space diagonalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24595)
*Jingyi Chao,Kun Xu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用两味Nambu-Jona-Lasinio（NJL）模型，在有限温度和外加磁场下研究带电赝标量（π⁺）和矢量（ρ⁺）介子的动力学与质量谱；通过引入分离Schwinger相位的夸克传播子，构建了基于Wigner-Weyl变换和Moyal星积的精确非对易相空间框架，实现了不对称分数组分电荷束缚态Bethe-Salpeter方程的代数对角化；结果表明π⁺质量严格跟随零点能漂移，满足广义Goldstone定理；ρ⁺自旋劈裂源于手性Dirac代数决定的微观阈值截断，且其自旋平行态的快子不稳定性被磁催化效应抑制；所有介子在手征对称性恢复前保持束缚态，无Mott解离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解强相互作用物质在强磁场与高温下的介子行为，特别是手征对称性破缺、Goldstone模式实现及矢量介子自旋劈裂等非微扰量子色动力学（QCD）效应。

Method: 采用两味NJL模型，构造含Schwinger相位分离的夸克传播子，结合Wigner-Weyl变换与Moyal星积建立非对易相空间框架，代数求解Bethe-Salpeter方程，并分析真空求和规则、零点能、Zeeman劈裂与热效应。

Result: π⁺极点质量严格追踪eB阶零点能漂移，满足广义Goldstone定理；ρ⁺出现动力学Zeeman自旋劈裂，但自旋平行态的tachyonic不稳定性被磁催化抑制；连续谱阈值2M随磁场升高而上移，阻止矢量介子凝聚；有限温度下介子质量单调下降，但未发生Mott解离。

Conclusion: 在NJL框架下，强磁场中赝标量与矢量介子的质量行为由手征结构、相空间非对易性与磁催化共同决定；π⁺作为广义Goldstone玻色子表现稳健，ρ⁺虽有Zeeman劈裂但不发生凝聚，且所有介子在手征恢复前保持束缚态。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamics and mass spectra of charged pseudoscalar ($π^+$) and vector ($ρ^+$) mesons in a background magnetic field at finite temperature using the two-flavor Nambu-Jona--Lasinio (NJL) model. By employing a quark propagator that isolates the Schwinger phase from its Landau level expansion, we formulate an exact non-commutative phase-space framework utilizing the Wigner-Weyl transform and the Moyal star product. This approach enables the algebraic diagonalization of the Bethe-Salpeter equations for composite states with asymmetric fractional constituent charges. For the pseudoscalar channel, we analytically verify the exact cancellation between the dynamical random phase approximation spatial sum rules and the vacuum gap equation. This identity preserves the generalized Goldstone theorem, causing the $π^+$ pole mass to strictly track the kinematic zero-point energy drift at order of $eB$. In the vector channel, our full phase-space evaluation reveals that the Zeeman spin-splitting emerges dynamically from microscopic threshold truncations governed by the chiral Dirac algebra. Notably, we find that the tachyonic instability of the spin-aligned $ρ^+$ state is quenched. The magnetic catalysis of the chiral condensate drives the continuum threshold ($2M$) upwards, overtaking the Zeeman attraction and preventing vector meson condensation within this mean-field framework. Furthermore, finite-temperature evaluations show a monotonic thermal suppression of the meson masses driven by Pauli blocking, yet all modes remain bound without undergoing Mott dissociation prior to chiral symmetry restoration.

### [26] [Nucleon decays into one lepton plus two non-strange mesons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24613)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 对15种含e⁺/μ⁺/ν̂与两个非奇异介子的三体衰变，给出迄今最强的部分寿命下限；其中带电轻子道比PDG限强逾三个数量级，5种中微子道首次给出Γ⁻¹≳10³⁴年；同时将n→e⁺π⁻、n→μ⁺π⁻、p→ν̂π⁺等两体道限制提升约2倍。

Abstract: Nucleon decays into a lepton and two pseudoscalar mesons represent key channels for probing baryon number violation, complementing conventional two-body modes. In this Letter, we model-independently correlate two- and three-body processes within the framework of low-energy effective field theory, performing a global analysis that avoids single-operator-dominance assumption. We derive significantly improved bounds on 15 three-body modes with a lepton ($e^+,\,μ^+,\hatν=ν/\barν$) and two non-strange mesons ($π,η$). For charged-lepton modes, our lower limits on partial lifetimes ($Γ^{-1}$) surpass current Particle Data Group (PDG) values by more than three orders of magnitude. For 5 (anti)neutrino modes, we establish for the first time $Γ^{-1}\gtrsim 10^{34}\,\rm yr$. Additionally, our analysis improves constraints on two-body processes $n\to e^+π^-$, $n\to μ^+π^-$, and $p\to \hatνπ^+$ by approximately a factor of 2 compared to the PDG limits. These results highlight the importance of leveraging correlations among different processes to better probe new physics, enabling more stringent constraints on experimentally challenging processes from well-measured ones.

### [27] [On the Two $R$-Factors in the Small-$x$ Shockwave Formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24629)
*Yuri V. Kovchegov,M. Gabriel Santiago,Huachen Sun*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出两种新理论方法，以消除小x区域强子物理中常用的两个R因子：一是通过修改偶极散射振幅的快度变量来处理非零纵向动量转移效应；二是通过修正初值条件和采用积分形式的非线性演化方程来包含弹性散射振幅的实部。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 消除小x区域唯象分析中依赖的两个经验性R因子（分别对应非零纵向动量转移和弹性振幅实部），提升理论自洽性与预测能力。

Method: 1) 将偶极振幅N和奇球振幅O的快度变量Y = ln(1/x)替换为Y = ln min{1/|x|, 1/|ξ|}，以纳入偏斜度ξ效应；2) 重新构造初值条件，并将非线性小x演化方程写成积分形式，从而自然导出实部Im N与Im O。

Result: 给出了可推广至广义部分子分布（GPD）和广义横动量依赖部分子分布（GTMD）的小x、小非零ξ区域的统一处理方案；实部贡献不再需额外R因子，而是由修正的初值与演化方程内在决定。

Conclusion: 所提出的两项理论改进有望完全取代现有唯象分析中的两个R因子，增强小x QCD演化框架的严格性与普适性。

Abstract: There are two $R$-factors frequently used in the phenomenology of exclusive processes at small values of the Bjorken $x$ variable. One $R$-factor takes into account the effects of non-zero longitudinal momentum transfer, which is assumed to be zero in the dipole scattering amplitude. Another $R$-factor accounts for the real part of the elastic scattering amplitude which is often neglected, with the standard dipole scattering amplitude giving only the imaginary part of the elastic amplitude.
  In this work we present two new theoretical developments aimed at eliminating the need for the two $R$-factors. We argue that the $R$-factors can be replaced by (i) modifying the argument of the dipole scattering amplitude and by (ii) augmenting the initial conditions for its non-linear small-$x$ evolution. Specifically, we show that to account for the effects of non-zero skewness $ξ$, one has to replace the rapidity argument $Y = \ln (1/x)$ of the eikonal dipole amplitude $N$ and the odderon dipole amplitude $\cal O$ by $Y = \ln \min \left\{ 1/|x|, 1/|ξ|\right\}$. The prescription applies to the elastic scattering cross sections, as well as for calculations of the Generalized Parton Distributions and Generalized Transverse Momentum Dependent parton distributions at small $x$ and at small but non-zero skewness $ξ$. We also show that the real part of the scattering amplitude, proportional to Im~$N$, which is intimately connected to the signature factor of the amplitude, can be accounted for by a more careful evaluation of the initial condition for the evolution and by writing the non-linear evolution equation in an integral form. One can similarly construct Im~$\cal O$ for the odd-signature odderon amplitude. We hope that future implementation of our prescriptions presented here will eliminate the need for both phenomenological $R$-factors.

</details>

These solutions have been constructed on a selection of manifolds having positive, negative, and vanishing spatial scalar curvatures. One example is shown to be indistinguishable locally from a homogeneous Friedman cosmological model, others are constructed with significant inhomogeneities. Together these examples are used to explore the strengths and the limitations of the numerical methods used in this study, and to test the code used to implement them.

### [29] [Assessing EMRI Detectability of the Rotating Quantum Oppenheimer-Snyder Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23163)
*Dan Zhang,Shulan Li,Guoyang Fu,Jian-Pin Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文评估了量子引力效应对极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）的影响，特别是在旋转量子Oppenheimer-Snyder（qOS）黑洞背景下；通过绝热演化计算引力波相位偏移，并利用增强解析拼接（AAK）波形分析不同自转参数a下含/不含量子参数α的波形保真度；结果表明LISA可探测到量子引力效应印记，但黑洞自转会抑制该信号，强调在利用EMRI探测量子引力时必须谨慎考虑旋转自由度。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探测量子引力效应，特别是通过极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）这一高精度引力波探针，并厘清黑洞旋转对量子修正信号的影响。

Method: 采用绝热演化方法计算量子修正参数α引起的引力波相位偏移；构建并使用增强解析拼接（AAK）波形模型；通过计算含/不含α的波形保真度来量化可探测性。

Result: 量子引力效应在LISA中产生可观测的相位印记；黑洞自转参数a越大，该印记越被抑制；保真度分析表明旋转显著削弱量子信号的可分辨性。

Conclusion: 在利用EMRI观测探测量子引力时，必须将黑洞旋转作为关键自由度纳入建模与数据分析，否则可能导致对量子效应的误判或漏检。

Abstract: This letter presents an assessment of quantum gravity effects on extreme-mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) for the rotating quantum Oppenheimer-Snyder (qOS) black hole. Employing the adiabatic evolution, we compute the gravitational wave (GW) dephasing, which quantifies the cumulative phase shift induced by the quantum correction α . We further generate the augmented analytic kludge (AAK) waveform and investigate the faithfulness between the waveforms with and without the quantum parameter α for different values of a. Our results reveal that the quantum gravity effect induces detectable imprints in LISA, while the presence of rotation suppresses these signatures. This suggests that rotational degrees of freedom must be carefully accounted for when probing quantum gravity with EMRI observations.

### [30] [Ground measurements of the gravitational redshift questioned:re-establishing the physical bases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23250)

Conclusion: Pound-Rebka实验在物理学中的地位得到确认和恢复，仍是验证广义相对论引力红移的关键实验证据。

Abstract: Motivated by alleged inconsistencies in the scientific and educational literature, Asenbaum, Overstreet and Kasevic \href{https://doi.org/10.1088/1402-4896/ad340c}{(2024)} aim to clarify some fundamental concepts in the physics of gravitation. To this end they reexamine the first experimental measurement of the gravitational redshift by Pound and Rebka in 1960, claiming that it did not in fact measure the gravitational redshift predicted by Einstein almost half a century earlier, but rather a Doppler shift originating from non-gravitational reaction forces. We show that their conclusion arises from a misunderstanding of the reference systems involved, along with an unphysical interpretation of non gravitational forces. Thus, our work restores the Pound and Rebka experiment to its rightful place in Physics.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The quasinormal mode spectrum is a unique fingerprint linking gravitational-wave observations to extra-dimensional geometry. In this Letter, we show that thick braneworlds exhibit a spectral butterfly effect: infinitesimal deformations of the effective potential trigger dramatic migrations of quasinormal modes, challenging the presumed stability of this fingerprint. Frequency-domain instabilities depend sensitively on the perturbation's location and strength. In the time domain, near-brane perturbations primarily modify the early ringdown, while far-brane perturbations generate clean late-time echoes. Crucially, the graviton zero mode remains localized, preserving four-dimensional gravity. Despite this pronounced spectral fragility, the observable early-stage signal under current detector sensitivities is still dominated by the original fundamental mode. Hence, thick braneworlds display a nontrivial coexistence of a fragile spectrum and a resilient ringdown, supporting the continued use of the standard fingerprint in present-day gravitational-wave astronomy while revealing its hidden sensitivity.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于Kerr时空的不变量结构，构造一个函数，使其零点对应于与所有光子面相切的特殊类光测地线；引入以洛伦兹参数（等效为轨道倾角）表征的不变量来标识球形光子轨道，并由此确定其运动常数；进一步推广至能层和局部视界等几何面的不变量识别。

Abstract: We present an invariant characterization of the Kerr spacetime, and utilize the invariant structure of the spacetime to derive a function whose zeros identify a special family of null geodesics. Each member of this family is tangent to every photon surface in the Kerr photon region, offering a method of invariantly characterizing photon surfaces in axially symmetric spacetimes and thereby a providing a computational tool for efficiently computing the geodesic equations for any part of the photon region. The invariant that identifies all of the spherical photon orbits is parameterized by a Lorentz parameter, where the parameter is effectively an inclination angle of the spherical photon orbits through the equatorial plane. We also show how the invariant determines the constants of motion for all spherical orbits in the photon region. Finally, we briefly derive invariants which identify the other geometrically important surfaces such as the ergosurfaces and local horizons.

We further investigate formation of trapped surfaces during the dynamical evolution of the collapsing body. {It is found} that for the obtained solutions, {the} trapped surface formation can be avoided and consequently, the bounce event is not covered by the apparent horizon. Abstract: Spectral problems governed by differential operators underpin a wide range of physical systems, yet remain computationally challenging because their spectra depend sensitively on continuous parameters and often demand repeated evaluations across parameter space. Here we present $\texttt{DeepOPiraKAN}$, an open source physics informed neural network architecture for spectral analysis. By combining operator learning with enhanced optimization stability, it captures the underlying parameter-to-spectrum mapping in a single model, avoiding repeated spectral solutions at isolated points in parameter space. As a representative and stringent benchmark, we apply this framework to the computation of quasinormal modes of Kerr black holes. A single trained network accurately resolves modes with $(\ell,m)\in \{(2,0),(2,1)\}$ and overtones up to $n=7$ across the full spin range, achieving relative errors of $\mathcal{O}(10^{-6})$ for the fundamental mode and gradually increasing to $\mathcal{O}(10^{-4})$ for higher overtones, benchmarked against the Leaver's method. This level of accuracy is already significant for black hole spectroscopy and practical ringdown modelling for current and future observatories. More broadly, these results highlight the potential of $\texttt{DeepOPiraKAN}$ as a general and scalable framework for parameter dependent spectral problems across complex physical systems.

### [36] [Stationary solutions in the small-$c$ expansion of GR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23677)

Abstract: We study the small-$c$ expansion of general relativity in ADM variables up to next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO). We show that, in the stationary sector, this formulation renders the field equations more tractable for explicit solution building. The stationary sector exhibits both strong- and weak-gravity branches, whose structure becomes richer at NNLO. In the strong-gravity branch, we first obtain exact vacuum solutions of NLO Carroll gravity, including the Lense--Thirring and rotating C-metric backgrounds. At NNLO, we then construct the corresponding Lense--Thirring-type and C-metric-type exact vacuum geometries. We further extend the $\ell=0,2$ sector by including higher multipoles up to $\ell=4$, where $\ell$ denotes the multipole index. These results show that the full NLO/NNLO theory admits a richer stationary vacuum sector than the magnetic Carroll truncation. More broadly, the ADM formulation provides a practical framework for constructing and analyzing stationary backgrounds in the small-$c$ expansion of general relativity, and may also offer a useful framework for organizing rotational and higher-multipole deformations relevant to compact astrophysical objects such as slowly rotating black holes and neutron stars.

### [38] [On gravitating dyonic configurations in nonlinear electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23741)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非线性电磁场在广义相对论中的精确解多限于纯电或纯磁情形，而同时含非零电荷与磁荷（dyonic）的解极为稀少；本文旨在拓展此类解的存在性与普适性，尤其面向更广义的引力理论框架。

Method: 基于球对称静态假设，分析Lagrangian为L(f)（其中f=F_μνF^μν）的非线性电磁场；聚焦等量电荷与磁荷（q_e = q_m）情形，利用f的不变性及Maxwell极限约束，推导f≡0的全局成立条件，并考察其在GR及扩展引力理论（如标量-张量、F(R)引力）中的适用性。

Result: 证明只要L(f)在弱场下正确还原为Maxwell理论，则必存在f=0的全域电磁场构型；由此导出的引力-电磁耦合解在GR（含其他物质源）及多种扩展引力理论中均精确成立且形式高度简化。

Conclusion: f=0构型是连接非线性电磁学与多种引力理论的一类普适、简洁解；该结果不仅丰富了dyonic黑洞与星体模型的理论基础，也为检验不同引力理论提供了新的可解基准。

Abstract: We consider static, spherically symmetric configurations of nonlinear electromagnetic fields with Lagrangians $L(f)$, where $f = F_{μν} F^{μν}$, in general relativity (GR) and other metric theories of gravity. The corresponding exact solutions are well known in the framework of GR in cases where only an electric charge ($q_e$) or a magnetic charge ($q_m$) are present, but only a few solutions in particular examples of $L(f)$ are known for dyonic systems with both nonzero $q_e$ and $q_m$. We study the properties of such systems in the special case of equal electric and magnetic charges and, assuming a correct Maxwell limit of $L(f)$, show that there always exists such a configuration of the electromagnetic field that the invariant $f$ is zero in the whole space. It leads to the existence of the corresponding families of solutions both in GR in the presence of other sources of gravity (like fluids or scalar fields) and in a wide range of extended theories of gravity (e.g., scalar-tensor and $F(R)$ gravity), in which the nonlinear electromagnetic field behaves in an especially simple manner.

</details>

The resulting constraints exhibit strong agreement with observations, with the model successfully describing the transition from decelerated to accelerated expansion. The evolution of the effective equation-of-state parameter, together with statefinder diagnostics and energy conditions, reveals a quintessence-like nature and confirms the physical viability of the model. Abstract: We investigate inflation in modified teleparallel gravity within a scalar-tensor framework. Inflation is driven by a string-inspired fiber inflation potential that naturally realizes a transient ultra slow-roll (USR) phase.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将黑洞度规视为满足$g_{tt}g_{rr}=-1$的Schwarzschild型度规，映射为二维可积有效稀释子理论的真空解，并关联到d维拟拓扑引力；利用积分运动方程的生成函数$f(r) = -g_{tt}$导出热力学质量，并采用Wald熵公式计算熵。

Result: 证明该生成函数直接给出广义第一定律中的热力学质量，Wald熵自然对应热力学熵；框架适用于各类视界拓扑及平直/AdS渐近、奇异/正则黑洞。

Conclusion: 该框架成功统一了多种d维静态黑洞的热力学描述，凸显了二维稀释子结构与高维黑洞热力学本质之间的深刻联系，为后续研究（如量子修正、相变）提供了几何与动力学基础。

Abstract: We present a unified framework for the discussion of black hole thermodynamics of $d$-dimensional static black holes with spherical, toroidal or compact hyperbolic horizon topology satisfying $g_{tt}g_{rr}=-1$ in Schwarzschild gauge. To that end, we consider any such black hole as a solution to an integrable $2$-dimensional effective dilaton theory and thereby as a vacuum solution to an extended notion of $d$-dimensional quasi-topological gravity. We show that the generating function determining $f(r) = -g_{tt} $ in the integrated equation of motion provides the thermodynamic mass in a generalised first law with entropy computed as the Wald entropy. The framework presented here can be applied to singular and regular black holes with flat or anti-de Sitter asymptotics.

Abstract: Effective field theory (EFT) provides a systematic framework to describe possible deviations from general relativity through higher-curvature corrections to the gravitational action, capturing low-energy effects of an underlying fundamental theory.
  In this work, we investigate quasinormal modes (QNMs) and both weak and strong gravitational lensing in static, spherically symmetric spacetimes, focusing on the behavior of null geodesics near the photon sphere. Adopting the strong deflection limit formalism developed by Bozza, we derive the logarithmic divergence structure of the deflection angle and explicitly separate the divergent and regular contributions.

We show that these quantities encode direct information about higher-curvature corrections to the gravitational action.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Asymptotic symmetries are expected to leave subtle but physically meaningful imprints on quantum probes of gravity, yet their manifestation in near-horizon dynamics remains incompletely understood. We examine this question for a closed bosonic string propagating in the near-horizon geometry of a five-dimensional Schwarzschild black hole subjected to a generalized Bondi-van der Burg-Metzner-Sachs (BMS) supertranslation. The extended nature of the string makes it especially sensitive to the resulting anisotropic geometric distortions, and this sensitivity appears most clearly in the angular sector of the worldsheet dynamics. Under the gauge and falloff conditions adopted here, the temporal and radial sectors remain unaffected by the supertranslation, while the angular deformation breaks the original SO(4) symmetry of the background. The radial equation is governed by modified Bessel modes, with a nonvanishing radial conserved current, indicating transport-like propagation. Radial squeezing driven by gravity and anisotropic angular spreading induced by supertranslations provide a dynamical realization of string spreading near the horizon. Thus this analysis demonstrates that probe string dynamics encodes nontrivial signatures of BMS-induced deformations, providing a dynamical probe of symmetry structures in higher-dimensional black hole spacetimes.

In this paradigm, gravity amounts to an effective causality deformation with respect to a more fundamental causality, which always encompasses the former through a causal cone hierarchy. In that paper, the fundamental idea was described in detail but fully elaborated only when restricted to the linear gravitational approximation. In this work, we discuss and conjecture how this idea could be extended to the full non-linear regime. Abstract: The space-borne gravitational-wave (GW) detectors will open a new mass and redshift regime, allowing us to observe massive black hole binaries (MBHBs) throughout the Universe. A subset of these systems is expected to produce electromagnetic (EM) counterparts, offering a unique opportunity to follow the continuous evolution of massive black holes through joint GW and EM observations. Realizing this potential, however, requires low-latency, high-throughput data-analysis pipelines that can extract reliable source parameters and sky localizations from space-borne data streams fast enough to trigger EM follow-up. In this work we develop a fast, normalising flow-based inference pipeline designed for early-warning analysis of MBHB signals in a TianQin-like configuration. Our method combines a learned embedding of the detector time series with a neural spline flow (NSF) to perform amortized Bayesian inference, producing posterior samples for the main source parameters in roughly one minute per event. For a representative MBHB whose merger occurs $\sim 15$ minutes after the end of the analyzed GW observation, the pipeline achieves pre-merger sky localizations of order $\sim 20~\mathrm{deg}^2$, recovers the same number of sky modes as a reference parallel-tempered Markov chain Monte Carlo (PTMCMC) analysis, and yields parameter uncertainties of comparable scale, while still operating within a practically useful pre-merger warning window. These results demonstrate that NSF-based inference can deliver accurate, near-real-time parameter estimation for space-borne MBHB GW signals, and that the resulting early-warning localizations are sufficiently precise to make rapid EM follow-up.

Method: 采用Padé改进的WKB方法计算拟正则频率，并用时域Prony方法对标量基模进行验证。

Result: 发现增大正则性参数会使拟正则模的振荡频率和阻尼率均减小，品质因子变化微弱；该谱移动显著强于数值不确定性。

Conclusion: DBI正则性尺度在黑洞ringdown谱中留下清晰、稳健且自旋依赖的印记，为通过引力波观测检验正则黑洞模型提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We study massless scalar, electromagnetic, and Dirac perturbations of the exact asymptotically flat regular black hole supported by a phantom Dirac--Born--Infeld scalar. Using the Padé-improved WKB method, with a time-domain Prony check for the scalar fundamental mode, we compute representative quasinormal frequencies and find that larger regularity shifts the spectrum toward smaller oscillation frequencies and damping rates, whereas the quality factor changes only weakly. The spectral shifts remain well above the estimated numerical uncertainty, demonstrating that the DBI regularity scale leaves a robust spin-dependent imprint on ringdown.

</details>


### [48] [Gravitational waves of extreme-mass-ratio inspirals in a rotating black hole with Dehnen dark matter halo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24413)
*Kun Meng,Shao-Jun Zhang,Nan Yang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）在Kerr黑洞和带有Dehnen型暗物质晕的旋转黑洞（DMBH）背景下的引力波辐射特性，通过Teukolsky形式框架和Sasaki-Nakamura变换求解扰动方程，并分析了暗物质晕对波形振幅与相位的影响及探测器中的可分辨性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于Newman-Penrose形式推导Teukolsky型曲率扰动方程，在Kerr和DMBH背景下分别分离变量得到径向与角向方程；应用Sasaki-Nakamura变换将Teukolsky方程转化为便于数值求解的形式；计算无穷远与视界处的能量和角动量通量以建模轨道演化；数值求解提取引力波两个偏振分量；结合探测器响应函数计算应变并评估Kerr与DMBH波形间的失配度。

Result: 暗物质晕导致EMRI引力波波形在振幅和相位上均出现明显变化；失配度随暗物质晕质量参数和中心黑洞自旋增大而增加，表明高精度波形建模对暗物质探测具有潜力。

Conclusion: Dehnen型暗物质晕会显著改变EMRI引力波波形特征，其效应可通过未来空间引力波探测器（如LISA）的波形匹配分析予以识别，从而为暗物质分布和黑洞周边环境提供新的天体物理探针。

Abstract: Extreme Mass Ratio Inspirals (EMRIs) are among the key targe sources for the space-based gravitational wave (GW) detectors. The waveforms of the EMRIs are highly sensitive to the types of the central supermassive black hole (SBH) and can serve as a novel sensitive tool to probe the background spacetime. In this work, we compute GWs radiated from EMRIs in the backgrounds of Kerr black hole and rotating black hole with Dehnen-type dark matter halo (DMBH). Following the Teukolsky prescription, we obtain the perturbed equations for curvature tensor from the Newman-Penrose (NP) equations, and for the DMBH we obtain the radial and angular equations through separation of variables. To solve the equations with numerical method we apply the Sasaki-Nakamura (SN) transformation to convert the Teykolsky-type equation into the SN equation. We study the radiation reaction of GWs by computing the energy flux and angular momentum flux at infinity and at the horizon. The orbital evolution is then derived from the total fluxes. We extract the two polarizations of GWs by solving the equation numerically. By comparing the waveforms of Kerr and DMBH, it is found that the DM halo induces noticeable changes in both the amplitude and phase of GWs. We compute the strain of GW detector with the response function and evaluate the mismatch between the waveforms of Kerr and DMBH. The results show that the mismatch increases with the mass parameter of DM halo and the spin of the SBH.

### [50] [Tests of scalar polarizations with multi-messenger events](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24526)
*Sk Md Adil Imam,Macarena Lagos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用GW170817引力波事件及伴随的电磁对应体（特别是伽马暴余辉的偏振角约束），在参数化后爱因斯坦框架（PPE）下对广义相对论进行检验，引入标量呼吸模与张量模修正，并结合四极（ℓ=|m|=2）和偶极（ℓ=|m|=1）谐波分析；结果表明四极模式下存在约2σ的标量模迹象，而偶极模式无此迹象，且电磁偏振角约束显著收紧了非GR参数限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义相对论仅预言两种张量偏振模式，而一般度规理论允许最多六种独立偏振模式；引力波观测为强场引力检验提供了独特机会，需结合多信使信息提升检验精度。

Method: 采用参数化后爱因斯坦（PPE）框架，扩展GR波形以包含标量呼吸模及张量模修正，引入三个非GR参数；结合GW170817的引力波数据与伽马暴余辉偏振角等电磁对应体信息，开展贝叶斯推断，分别针对四极（ℓ=|m|=2）和偶极（ℓ=|m|=1）角动量模式、两种频率演化模型进行分析。

Result: 在ℓ=|m|=2模式下，标量模振幅偏离零约2σ，呈现弱偏好；在ℓ=|m|=1模式下无此偏好；电磁偏振角约束大幅收紧非GR参数限制——例如ℓ=|m|=2情形下，标量（张量）振幅修正参数的限制分别提升约60%（30%）。

Conclusion: 多信使联合分析（尤其是长期电磁后随观测提供的偏振角约束）可显著增强引力理论检验能力；当前结果虽未否定广义相对论，但提示在特定模式下存在偏离可能，支持进一步高精度多信使检验。

Abstract: Gravitational wave (GW) observations provide a unique opportunity to test Einstein's General Relativity (GR) in the strong-field regime. While GR predicts only two tensor polarization modes, generic metric theories allow up to six independent modes. We perform a parameterized test of GR using the parameterized post-Einsteinian (PPE) framework applied to GW170817, incorporating for the first time the polarization angle constraints from the gamma-ray burst afterglow alongside other electromagnetic (EM) counterpart information. We extend the GR waveform by adding a scalar breathing mode and modifications to the tensor modes, introducing three non-GR parameters. We perform Bayesian inference for both quadrupole $\ell = |m|= 2$ and dipole $\ell = |m|= 1$ angular harmonics, with two frequency evolution models. For $\ell = |m|= 2$ , we find mild preference for a scalar mode (scalar amplitude deviates from zero at $\sim 2 σ$), while for the $\ell = |m|= 1$, we find no preference for a scalar mode. The EM constraint on the polarization angle places very tight bounds on non-GR parameters; for instance, in the case $\ell = |m| = 2$, the bound on the scalar (tensor) amplitude modification parameter improves by roughly $60\%$ $(30\%)$, highlighting the impact that long-term follow up of GW events can have on tests of gravity.

### [51] [Pair-Dependent Drift of Kerr Neighboring-Overtone Gap Minima](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24584)
*Yuye Wu,Hong-Bo Jin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究克尔黑洞的准正规模（QNMs）随自旋参数变化时相邻高阶模之间的复频率间隙，发现其存在鲁棒的内部极小值，且极小值位置随模对变化而漂移；作者将该问题重构为复分离量的局部零点问题，并提出一个无分母的实投影诊断量来刻画极小值，进而给出几何解释：极小值对应分离矢量的局部径向转向事件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高阶准正规模在黑洞 ringdown 早期起作用，且相邻模式在复频率平面上可能呈现局域组织结构，因此需系统研究其随黑洞自旋连续变化的行为，特别是相邻高阶模之间的复频率间隙。

Method: 通过沿自旋参数连续追踪克尔黑洞的准正规模，分析同一(s,ℓ,m)扇区中相邻高阶模的复频率间隙；将极小值条件重构为复分离量的局部零点问题；引入一个分母自由的实投影诊断量（即复分离量与其自旋导数共轭乘积的实部），并据此分析极小值漂移机制；辅以扩展但受限的代表性模集验证局部图像。

Result: 发现复频率间隙存在鲁棒的内部极小值，其自旋位置在不同模对间发生漂移；该漂移可归因于所提实投影诊断量主导零点的漂移；极小值具有清晰几何含义——对应复平面上分离矢量的局部径向转向（radial turning event），而角向运动仍可存在；所提局部图像在所检验的触发情形中成立，但具体零点环境本质上依赖于模对。

Conclusion: 准正规模相邻高阶模间的复频率间隙极小值并非固定于某自旋值，而是动态漂移的，其本质是复分离量在自旋演化中经历的局部径向转向；该现象可通过新提出的实投影诊断量定量刻画，支持了对黑洞谱精细结构的局域、几何化理解。

Abstract: Quasinormal modes (QNMs) underpin black-hole ringdown modeling and spectroscopy, where higher overtones can contribute at early times and neighboring modes can become locally organized in the complex-frequency plane. Motivated by this, we continuously track Kerr overtones along a spin scan and study a raw neighboring-overtone quantity: the complex-frequency gap between adjacent overtones. We find robust interior minima whose spin locations drift from pair to pair, even within the same \((s,\ell,m)\) sector. We explain this by reformulating minimum setting as a local zero-setting problem for the complex separation between the two modes. Differentiating the squared gap yields a denominator-free real-projection diagnostic (the real part of the product between the complex separation, with conjugation, and its spin derivative). The sampled minimum is governed by an approximate local zero of this diagnostic, so minimum drift becomes the drift of its dominant zero crossing. This also yields a geometric picture: the minimum is a local radial turning event of the separation vector, while angular motion in the complex plane may persist. Finally, an expanded but deliberately restricted representative set (including same-family continuations, external positive transfers, and smooth no-trigger controls) supports this local picture for the triggered cases examined here. At the same time, the detailed local crossing environment remains intrinsically pair dependent.

### [52] [Hawking Temperature, Sparsity and Energy Emission Rate of Dark Matter Halo Regular Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24659)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Edilberto O. Silva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了由Einasto密度剖面描述的暗物质晕所源起的正则黑洞的热力学和辐射性质，发现暗物质晕会抑制霍金温度和能量辐射率，并导致比标准黑洞更高的稀疏性参数，同时特定热容在有限视界半径范围内可为正，表明存在热力学稳定相及Davies型相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究暗物质晕（以Einasto密度剖面描述）对正则黑洞热力学与辐射性质的影响，拓展黑洞物理与暗物质理论的交叉研究。

Method: 推导霍金温度、比热容、霍金辐射稀疏参数及能谱辐射率的闭式表达式，并将其作为暗物质分布特征尺度参数α的函数进行分析，与标准Schwarzschild黑洞结果对比。

Result: 暗物质晕抑制霍金温度和能量辐射率；比热容在有限视界半径区间内为正，预示热力学稳定相及Davies型相变；稀疏参数高于标准黑洞，表明霍金辐射更间歇。

Conclusion: 暗物质环境显著改变黑洞热力学稳定性与辐射特性，为理解暗物质与黑洞相互作用提供了新视角。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the thermodynamic and radiative properties of a regular black hole sourced by a dark matter halo described by the Einasto density profile. The closed-form expressions for the Hawking temperature, specific heat capacity, sparsity parameter of Hawking flux, and the spectral energy emission rate were obtained. All these are examined as a function of the characteristic scale parameter $α$ of the dark matter distribution and compared with the standard Schwarzschild results. We show that the presence of a dark matter halo suppresses both the Hawking temperature and energy emission rate relative to the standard black hole result. Crucially, the specific heat capacity can be positive for a finite range of horizon radii, signaling a thermodynamically stable phase; the boundary of this stable region defines a Davies-type phase transition. The sparsity parameter is higher than in the standard black hole, indicating that the dark matter environment makes the Hawking flux even more intermittent.

### [53] [Semiclassical phases of charged spin-$1/2$ matter-wave interferometers in gravitational wave backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24751)
*Nontapat Wanwieng,Apimook Watcharangkool*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于协变狄拉克方程WKB展开的半经典框架，用于分析带电自旋-1/2物质波干涉仪在弯曲时空（特别是引力波背景）中的相位响应，将总相位分解为动力学、自旋和电磁Aharonov-Bohm三部分，并指出它们均由局部潮汐场支配且具有不同物理耦合机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解引力波如何通过时空曲率影响量子干涉，尤其需统一描述物质波干涉仪中多种相位贡献（动力学、自旋、电磁）的起源与耦合机制。

Method: 基于协变狄拉克方程进行WKB展开，构建适用于带电自旋-1/2粒子的半经典干涉理论；在自由下落参考系中分析相位构成；结合弯曲时空中的麦克斯韦方程推导曲率诱导的电磁场。

Result: 发现动力学相位、自旋相位和AB相位均受同一潮汐尺度$\ddot{h}_A \sim Ω^2_{gw}h_0$调控，并共享几何核函数；AB相位不仅依赖磁通，还依赖诱导电磁场的空间变化及干涉臂 traversal 时间决定的固有频率响应。

Conclusion: 该框架为引力波背景下物质波干涉提供了统一相位描述，揭示了时空曲率通过动力学、自旋和电磁三种互补通道对量子干涉施加影响。

Abstract: A matter wave propagating through curved spacetime accumulates phase that encodes both geometry and gauge structure. We develop a semiclassical framework for charged spin-$1/2$ matter-wave interferometers based on a WKB expansion of the covariant Dirac equation, in which the phase decomposes into dynamical, spin, and electromagnetic Aharonov-Bohm (AB) contributions. In a freely falling detector frame, all three channels are governed by local tidal fields. In a weak gravitational-wave (GW) background, the dynamical and spin phases probe the gravitoelectric and gravitomagnetic sectors of curvature, while the AB phase arises from curvature-induced electromagnetic fields obtained from Maxwell's equations in curved spacetime. For a Mach-Zehnder interferometer (MZI), all three responses are determined by the same tidal scale, $\ddot{h}_A \sim Ω^2_{gw}h_0$, and filtered by a common geometric kernel, while entering through distinct physical couplings. In particular, the AB contribution depends not only on the enclosed flux but also on spatial variations of the induced fields and exhibits an intrinsic frequency dependence set by the traversal time. These results provide a unified description of matter-wave interferometric phases in time-dependent GW backgrounds and identify complementary dynamical, spin, and electromagnetic pathways through which spacetime curvature imprints itself on quantum interference.

*Gert Aarts,Dénes Sexty*

Main category: hep-lat

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 系统综述了多种应对符号问题的理论与数值方法，包括全纯延拓（Lefschetz胎膜、全纯流、复路径变形、复Langevin）、新自由度引入（对偶变量、张量重正化群）以及新兴的机器学习方法，并评估其在简化模型与真实格点QCD中的适用性。

Conclusion: 尽管符号问题仍未彻底解决，但多条技术路线已展现出可控或缓解的潜力；未来需加强方法在真实QCD系统中的验证与协同优化。

Abstract: The sign problem obstructs the determination of the QCD phase diagram in the temperature-baryon chemical potential plane using lattice QCD. We review the sign problem in QCD and related field theories, including applications to real-time dynamics. We focus on approaches where the sign problem can potentially be solved or controlled, irrespective of its severeness. These include holomorphic extensions -- Lefschetz thimbles, holomorphic flow, contour deformations, and complex Langevin dynamics --, and the introduction of new degrees of freedom -- dual variables and the tensor renormalisation group. We also highlight directions in which machine learning approaches have shown promise. Since many methods are first tested in simpler models, we provide an outlook on their feasibility for lattice systems.

### [55] [The abundance and radial distribution of faint and ultra-faint dwarfs in galaxy clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22920)
*Pradyumna Sadhu,Laura V. Sales,Julio F. Navarro,Raphaël Errani,Jose Benavides,Eric W. Peng*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文结合TNG50宇宙学模拟与高分辨率N体模拟校准的经验潮汐演化模型，克服数值分辨率限制，预测大质量星系团内存在数千个超暗矮星系，并指出观测中因亮度/质量阈值导致内区严重剥离星系被遗漏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙学模拟（如TNG50）受限于数值分辨率，无法分辨矮星系，导致暗物质子结构被人工破坏，需更可靠方法研究星系团中矮星系的真实分布与演化。

Method: 将TNG50的ΛCDM流体动力学模拟结果与基于高分辨率理想化N体模拟校准的经验潮汐演化模型相结合，应用于TNG50中三个最重星系团，推断低于原模拟分辨率极限的矮星系性质。

Result: 在z=0时，M200~10^14 M⊙星系团内存在2000–7000个恒星质量>100 M⊙的矮星系，其整体径向分布匹配宿主暗物质轮廓；但观测常用的质量或光度下限会系统性剔除内区高度剥离的矮星系。

Conclusion: 该模型揭示了当前宇宙学模拟对矮星系统计的显著低估，强调未来Euclid、Rubin和Roman等巡天对验证星系团中超暗矮星系真实丰度与空间分布的关键作用。

Abstract: Cosmological simulations of galaxy clusters are unable to resolve dwarf galaxies due to limited numerical resolution which drives the artificial disruption of dark matter substructures. We address these limitations by combining the results of the cosmological hydrodynamical simulation TNG50 in $Λ$CDM with an empirical model of tidal evolution of cluster galaxies calibrated using high-resolution idealized N-body simulations. Applied to the three most massive clusters in TNG50, our model allows us to study the stellar mass and radial distribution of dwarfs well below the formal resolution limit of the parent simulation. We find that, at $z=0$, clusters with virial mass $M_{200} \sim 10^{14}~\mathrm{M_\odot}$ host a vast population of dwarf galaxies within the virial radius, amounting to $2000$-$7000$ systems with $M_* > 100~\mathrm{M_\odot}$. Taken together, these satellites follow a radial distribution that matches the underlying dark matter profile of the host. However, applying a minimum mass or luminosity threshold for detection, as expected in observational studies, tends to exclude the most heavily-stripped objects, which tend to populate the inner regions. Future surveys targeting ultra-faint galaxies in group and cluster environments, such as those made possible by the Euclid, Rubin, or Roman telescopes, will be fundamental to refute or confirm this prediction.

### [56] [Cluster-green galaxy correlations: where do these galaxies live?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22921)
*Selene Levis,Facundo Rodriguez,Héctor J. Martínez,Valeria Coenda,Hernán Muriel*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文研究了绿谷（GV）星系在星系系统中的空间分布，发现它们更倾向于存在于星系团外围，并作为卫星星系受环境淬灭影响而处于恒星形成向宁静态过渡阶段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 绿谷星系被认为是恒星形成星系与宁静星系之间的过渡种群，但其在大尺度环境中的空间分布及环境对星系淬灭的影响尚不明确。

Method: 利用Illustris TNG300-1数值模拟和SDSS观测数据，通过星系团-星系交叉相关函数（CCF）分析GV星系的空间分布；使用质量阈值log(M200/M⊙)≥13.5的星系系统作为中心，蓝、绿、红星系作为示踪体；并构建匹配SDSS选择函数的TNG模拟星表以检验投影效应。

Result: TNG模拟显示GV星系相对比例随离心距离增加而上升，在外围达峰值（尤其对低质量星系和暗晕），部分情况下甚至超过红星系比例；SDSS观测呈现类似趋势但GV比例始终低于红星系；匹配选择函数的模拟星表成功复现观测信号，表明差异主要源于投影效应。

Conclusion: GV星系偏好分布在星系系统外围，多为受中心暗晕束缚的卫星星系，支持其作为受环境淬灭影响的过渡态星系的观点。

Abstract: Green valley (GV) galaxies are thought to represent a transitional population between star-forming and quiescent systems. However, their spatial distribution relative to galaxy systems remains unclear, particularly in relation to the large-scale environmental influence on galaxy quenching. We aim to determine whether GV galaxies preferentially inhabit specific environments within galaxy systems. We analyse the spatial distribution of GV galaxies using the cluster-galaxy cross-correlation function (CCF), based on the hydrodynamical simulation Illustris TNG300-1 (TNG) and observational data from the Sloan Digital Sky Survey (SDSS). Galaxy systems with $\log(M_{200}/M_{\odot}) \geq 13.5$ are used as cluster centres, while galaxies classified as blue, green, or red serve as tracers for the correlation analysis. In TNG, GV galaxies show an increasing relative fraction with cluster-centric distance, peaking in the outskirts, particularly for low-mass galaxies and haloes, and in some cases the GV fraction exceeds that of red galaxies. SDSS data reveal qualitatively similar trends, with the GV fraction remaining below that of red galaxies at all scales. Mock catalogues built from TNG and matched to SDSS selection functions reproduce the observational signal, indicating that projection effects drive the differences between datasets. GV galaxies preferentially reside in the outskirts of galaxy systems as satellites bound to the central halo, supporting a scenario in which they are transitioning objects influenced by environmental quenching.

### [57] [Supermassive stars with embedded stellar black hole cores: dense assembling star clusters as faint multiple Little Red Dot systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22924)
*Antti Rantala*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过直接数值模拟，研究了高红移致密星团中极端质量恒星（EMSs）和超大质量恒星（SMSs）形成过程中，恒星级黑洞（BHs）如何被嵌入其气体包层，形成类星体（QS）相，并可能产生引力波源及与JWST观测到的微弱‘小红点’（LRDs）相关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用包含后牛顿黑洞动力学与恒星演化的直接星团组装数值模拟，分析高面密度（Σ_h ≳ 10⁶ M⊙ pc⁻²）环境下黑洞与EMSs/SMSs的相互作用。

Result: 发现恒星级黑洞可在质量分异与弛豫作用下嵌入EMSs/SMSs气体层，形成寿命远长于SMS本身的类星体（QS）相；该相支持持续吸积增长，并可形成多黑洞引力波源；QS参数（尺度~100 pc、质量≳10⁴ M⊙、邻近蓝星团）与JWST发现的微弱小红点（LRDs）一致。

Conclusion: QS相是致密星团中EMSs/SMSs形成过程的自然产物，为IMBH前身、延展质量增长及可探测引力波源提供了新通道，并可能解释JWST观测到的小红点天体。

Abstract: Numerical simulations have established that star clusters with densities comparable to the high redshift ($z>6$-$10$) James Webb Space Telescope (JWST) proto globular clusters may build up extremely massive (EMSs; $m_\mathrm{\star}>1000 M_\odot$) or even supermassive stars (SMSs; $m_\mathrm{\star}>10000 M_\odot$) and potentially intermediate mass black holes (IMBHs) through runaway stellar collisions. Using direct simulations of assembling star clusters including post-Newtonian black hole dynamics and stellar evolution, we demonstrate that in such dense environments ($Σ_\mathrm{h} \gtrsim 10^6 M_\odot$pc$^\mathrm{-2}$) stellar BHs ($m_\bullet \lesssim 60 M_\odot$), driven by rapid mass segregation and relaxation effects within the sphere of influence of the EMSs/SMSs, may strongly interact with the extremely massive stars and become embedded within their gaseous layers. We suggest that this quasi-star (QS) like embedded BH phase is a natural outcome of the runaway formation of EMSs/SMSs in the densest star clusters. The QS phase is orders of magnitude longer in duration than the lifetime of the SMS, enabling an extended growth period by stellar collisions, and allows the formation of embedded gravitational wave sources if the QS captures more than a single stellar BH. The star cluster assembly region sizes ($\sim100$ pc), QS masses ($\gtrsim 10^4 M_\odot$) and their proximity to young, massive blue star forming clumps are consistent with the faint population of multiple little red dots (LRDs) recently discovered by the JWST.

### [58] [Itô tracers: continuous-trajectory Lagrangian particles for Eulerian hydrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23041)
*Eric R. Moseley,R. Teyssier,Tom Abel*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新型连续时间拉格朗日示踪粒子——Itô示踪器，其统计矩与气体的对流、扩散和弥散相匹配，并在多个测试中显著优于传统及蒙特卡洛示踪器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统拉格朗日示踪粒子因仅依赖网格中心速度而忽略数值扩散，导致系统性偏差；蒙特卡洛示踪器虽能解决该问题，但轨迹在时间上不连续。本文旨在设计一种既物理准确又数学上连续的示踪方法。

Method: 提出Itô示踪器，基于匹配气体输运（对流、扩散、弥散）统计矩的随机微分方程；进一步构造子网格尺度变体SGS-Itô，用Smagorinsky-Lilly湍流扩散率替代数值扩散；通过1D方波平流和3D衰减湍流测试验证，并采用多种统计量（柱密度图、联合密度直方图、对数密度比PDF、密度功率谱）进行比较。

Result: Itô示踪器在各项统计指标上整体优于或等同于MC示踪器：在湍流测试中，其与气体的相关性提升>3%，对数密度比PDF宽度缩减近50%；相较经典示踪器，提升分别达≥30%和230%；且支持方差缩减、高阶积分器和GPU加速等优势。

Conclusion: Itô示踪器是一种更准确、更通用的连续时间拉格朗日示踪方法，不仅改善了统计保真度，还为扩展至尘埃、带电粒子、宇宙线等其他连续轨迹过程提供了统一框架。

Abstract: Lagrangian tracer particles have long been used to track the history of individual gas parcels in hydrodynamical codes. Particles advected by the cell-centered velocity carry no representation of underlying numerical diffusion, and thus exhibit systematic bias. The Monte-Carlo (MC) tracer resolves this with discrete probabilistic cell-to-cell, flux-based jumps, at the cost of trajectories that are discontinuous in time. We introduce the Itô tracer, a continuous-time Lagrangian particle with moments matched to the advection, diffusion, and dispersion of the gas. A subgrid-scale variant (SGS-Itô) replaces the numerical diffusion with a Smagorinsky--Lilly turbulent diffusivity, illustrating that the form of the diffusion matters less than its magnitude. We validate these methods with a 1D square-pulse advection test and 3D decaying turbulence at $σ_{\rm rms} = 15\,c_{\rm s}$. We compare the different tracer particle methods using several statistical tests. Itô tracers largely reproduce or improve upon MC tracers statistics across column-density maps, joint density histograms, log-density-ratio PDFs, and density power spectra. In the turbulence test, Itô tracers improve the correlation between tracers and gas over the MC tracers by >3\%, and reduce the width of the log-density ratio PDF by nearly 50\%. Relative to classical tracers, these improvements are $\gtrsim$30\% and 230\%, respectively. Because Itô tracers follow a stochastic differential equation, the method maps onto other continuous-trajectory Lagrangian processes (e.g. dust grains, charged particles, cosmic rays), admits variance-reduction techniques, higher-order integrators, and GPU-friendly implementations -- all of which are unavailable to discrete-jump schemes.

</details>

Abstract: A rare multiple open cluster system has been analyzed using Gaia DR3 astrometry and photometry data. Membership probabilities are refined through statistical modeling, combining GUMM, Bayesian-KDE, and Bayesian-XDGMM for tidal tails identification. Backward orbital integrations confirm coherent motions over 20-30 million years, suggesting a common origin from the same massive molecular cloud. ### [60] [Hessian-based photometric substructure as an evolutionary tracer of OB cluster candidates in M31](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23118)
*Yuan Liang,Chao-Wei Tsai,Jingwen Wu*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用哈勃太空望远镜图像构建了747个OB星团候选体新目录，并提出一种基于Hessian矩阵的无量纲结构度量CV_tr，发现其与星团年龄在紫外和蓝波段存在显著负相关，表明星团光分布随演化逐渐平滑，证实二阶测光结构可提供可观测的演化信息（~10–300 Myr）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统星团研究多依赖颜色-星等图（CMD）定龄，但对部分分辨星团，其内部光度子结构可能蕴含独立演化信息；需发展新指标量化该结构并检验其与年龄的关系。

Method: 基于PHAT/PHAST巡天的哈勃图像，构建747个OB星团候选体目录；定义迹系数变异率（CV_tr）作为结构指标，源自四波段Hessian矩阵；与具有CMD年龄估计的M31星团交叉匹配；采用bootstrap抽样验证统计显著性；并通过合成星团前向建模检验CV_tr–年龄关系的可靠性。

Result: 在UV和蓝波段发现CV_tr与年龄存在统计显著的负相关；bootstrap证实趋势稳健；前向建模在简化物理假设下成功复现单调CV_tr–年龄关系。

Conclusion: 二阶测光结构（以CV_tr表征）在CMD标定的年龄范围（~10–300 Myr）内携带可观测的星团演化信息，为部分分辨星团提供了新的、独立于CMD的演化诊断工具。

Abstract: Using \textit{Hubble Space Telescope} images from the PHAT and PHAST surveys, we construct an updated catalogue of 747 OB cluster (OBC) candidates. We introduce a dimensionless structural metric, the trace coefficient of variation ($CV_{\rm tr}$), derived from the Hessian matrix in four \textit{HST} bands, to quantify the internal photometric substructure of partially resolved OBC candidates. Cross-matching with the subset of M31 clusters that have independent colour--magnitude diagram (CMD) age estimates yields 247 objects in common. We find statistically significant anti-correlations between $CV_{\rm tr}$ and age in the UV and blue bands, suggesting a progressive smoothing of the light distribution as clusters evolve. Bootstrap resampling confirms the robustness of these trends. Forward modelling of synthetic clusters analysed with the same pipeline recovers a monotonic $CV_{\rm tr}$--age relation under simplified but physically motivated assumptions. These results show that second-order photometric structure contains measurable evolutionary information within the CMD-calibrated regime ($\sim10$--300~Myr).

### [61] [The Dependence of the Mean Spectral Energy Distributions on the Accretion Rate for Quasars with $z < 0.75$ from the Sloan Digital Sky Survey](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23123)
*Yan-Song Ma,Yu-Meng Guan,Jian-Xia Jiang,Shao-Jun Li,Xiang-Wei Ning,Yi Tang,Wei-Hao Bian*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文基于SDSS DR16中56969个z<0.75的类星体，构建了从紫外到中红外的平均谱能量分布（SED），发现SED形状与Eddington比、Fe II强度及Hβ线宽密切相关，揭示了吸积率和几何取向对AGN连续谱的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解类星体平均谱能量分布（SED）如何随基本物理参数（如Eddington比、Fe II强度、Hβ线宽）变化，以揭示AGN中心引擎与尘埃环等结构的物理联系。

Method: 利用SDSS DR16中56969个低红移类星体的多波段数据（MIR至UV），按eigenvector 1参数（R_FeII和FWHM_Hβ）及Eddington比（L_Bol/L_Edd）分组，构建多组平均SED并比较其连续谱形状。

Result: 发现R_FeII越大或L_Bol/L_Edd越高，UV/NIR/MIR连续谱越红（尘埃贡献增强）；但光学连续谱反而变蓝（更硬），显示光学区复杂性；FWHM_Hβ越大，MIR越蓝，暗示视线与尘埃环平面夹角增大导致MIR尘埃辐射减弱。

Conclusion: Type 1 AGN的SED形状系统性依赖于吸积率（L_Bol/L_Edd）和发射线特征（R_FeII、FWHM_Hβ），支持吸积物理与尘埃环几何共同塑造连续谱的观点。

Abstract: We construct mean spectral energy distributions (SEDs) for a substantial sample of 56,969 Sloan Digital Sky Survey DR16 quasars with $z < 0.75$, utilizing multiwavelength data from the mid-infrared (MIR) to ultraviolet (UV). These SEDs are built on eigenvector 1 parameters -- the relative optical $\rm Fe~ II$ strength ($R_{\rm Fe~II}$) and the H$β$ line width ($\rm Hβ$) -- that capture the principal spectral variance of quasar spectra. From three $R_{\rm Fe~II}$-dependent mean SEDs we find that quasars with a larger $R_{\rm Fe~II}$ exhibit redder UV and optical and redder MIR and near-infrared (NIR) continua, indicating more dust emission. We also split our sample directly into Eddington ratio $L_{\rm Bol} /L_{\rm Edd}$ (or dimensionless accretion rate $\dot{\mathscr{M}}$) bins to construct different mean SEDs and find that the continua become increasingly red with increasing $L_{\rm Bol} /L_{\rm Edd}$ (or $\dot{\mathscr{M}}$) in the MIR, NIR, and UV bands. This demonstrates that the shapes of Type 1 AGN SEDs depend on the accretion rate. However, the optical continuum shows the opposite trend (becoming harder and bluer), indicating the complexity of the optical emission region. From $\rm FWHM_{Hβ}$-dependent mean SEDs we find that quasars with a larger $\rm FWHM_{Hβ}$ show redder optical and NIR continua and bluer UV and MIR continua. The bluer MIR continuum suggests that a larger angle between of the line of sight and the torus plane results in weaker torus emission in the MIR.

*Xuejie Li,Zhongxu Zhai,Xiaohu Yang,Andrew Benson,Yun Wang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建条件图神经网络代理模型，融合Uchuu模拟的暗物质晕并合树与Galacticus SAM参数，预测多红移（z=0–5）下的星系性质。
